### [148] [NeuroCommitSSM: Decision-Centric Shared Autonomy for Safe Assistive Manipulation via EEG-EMG-ET Commit Readiness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15395)
*Tipu Sultan,Param Sangani,Kody Cool,Pascal Sikorski,Guangping Liu,Hadi Akbarpour,Madi Babaiasl*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: NeuroCommitSSM是一个面向辅助机器人操作的决策中心框架，通过融合脑电图、肌电图和眼动追踪信号预测连续就绪度分数，并结合三级状态机实现安全的"提交-执行"控制。在32名受试者、5种日常生活任务的实验中，该框架实现了0.950的动作平衡准确率，每1000个REST窗口仅产生0.75次误提交事件，且在传感器缺失场景下仍保持稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在辅助机器人操作中，现有系统通常关注"做什么"而非"何时执行"，缺乏决策时刻的安全控制机制。用户意图的准确时机判断对于防止误操作和提升人机协作安全性至关重要。

Method: 提出NeuroCommitSSM框架：(1) 从同步EEG/EMG/眼动追踪信号预测连续就绪度分数c_t∈[0,1]；(2) 通过滞回滤波和驻留时间阈值将连续分数转化为离散提交事件；(3) 设计HOLD-ASSIST-COMMIT三级有限状态监督器，在启动运动前要求同时满足神经模型持续就绪信号、目标可见性、逆运动学可解性和无碰撞规划等可行性条件。

Result: 在32名受试者、5种ADL任务上，LOSO交叉验证得到0.950动作平衡准确率，0.75 FP/1k REST。EEG-only条件下达0.785平衡准确率、0.29 FP/1k REST，而TCN基线在该条件下产生99.95 FP/1k REST。在Kinova Gen3机械臂上的硬件在环验证表明，可行性检查减少了误启动和决策不稳定。

Conclusion: NeuroCommitSSM通过神经信号驱动的决策时机建模与可行性校验的结合，显著降低了辅助机器人的误操作率，在传感器缺失场景下仍保持鲁棒性，为安全人机协同操作提供了有效方案。

Abstract: We present NeuroCommitSSM, a decision-centric framework that models when to execute, not just what to do, for safe commit-to-execute control in assistive robotic manipulation. NeuroCommitSSM predicts a continuous commit-readiness score c_t in [0,1] from synchronized electroencephalography (EEG), electromyography (EMG), and eye-tracking (ET), and converts it into discrete commit events through dwell and hysteresis filtering. A three-state finite-state supervisor, HOLD-ASSIST-COMMIT (HAC), gates execution by requiring both a sustained commit-readiness signal from the neural model and real-time perception and robot-state feasibility, including target visibility, inverse kinematics solvability, and collision-free planning, before initiating motion. We evaluate the framework on N=32 subjects performing five activities of daily living (ADL) tasks aligned with the International Classification of Functioning, Disability and Health (ICF), using leave-one-subject-out (LOSO) cross-validation and seven sensor-dropout scenarios (S0-S6). NeuroCommitSSM achieves 0.950 action-balanced accuracy with 0.75 false commit events per 1000 REST windows (FP/1k REST), and maintains low false commits and stable state transitions under sensor loss. For example, in the EEG-only condition, it achieves 0.785 balanced accuracy and 0.29 FP/1k REST, whereas the Temporal Convolutional Network baseline produces 99.95 FP/1k REST under the same condition. Hardware-in-the-loop (HIL) validation on a Kinova Gen3 arm shows that feasibility-checked execution reduces false starts and decision instability without sacrificing task success. Supplementary materials, including code, datasets, videos, and additional analyses, are available at https://madibabaiasl.github.io/NeuroCommitSSM/.

</details>

Method: 采用两部分浇铸法制造软体气动执行器，提出了防止内腔堵塞和确保气密密封的工艺；嵌入薄膜柔性传感器并标定；进行有限元建模（FEM）分析应力与变形；开展PID压力控制气动实验，结合自动化图像处理校准传感器，进行阶梯和正弦曲线驱动实验验证。

Various fabrication methods have been introduced, but many are labor-intensive and prone to human error. Therefore, traditional two-part pour casting remains an attractive option. This paper presents procedures for robust, repeatable, and scalable fabrication of soft pneumatic actuators using two-part pour casting. The presented methods prevent internal cavity clogging and ensure air-tight sealing. Additionally, a robust sensor embedding procedure for thin-film flex sensors is presented, which allows for accurate and repeatable data acquisition. Finite Element Modeling (FEM) of the soft actuator is performed to analyze stress and deformation from internal pressure loadings. Staircase and sinusoidal profile actuation experiments validate the performance of the fabricated actuator. Angle response experiments for the staircase input show repeatable performance, and the sinusoidal input shows a small amount of hysteresis consistent with viscoelastic response to pneumatic actuation of soft actuators. Simulated and real-world bending angles show comparable response. These methods provide a repeatable and robust fabrication procedure, validated across two operators and 24 successful fabrications, along with benchmark simulations and experimental testing. These benchmarks will enable more widespread adoption of soft robotics.

### [151] [Risk-Aware Preference Learning for Stochastic Outcomes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15483)
*Yi-Shiuan Tung,Yuni Wu,Wei Jiang,Alessandro Roncone,Bradley Hayes*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文研究人类风险敏感性对机器人奖励学习的影响，比较了期望效用理论和累积前景理论在社交机器人导航中的表现，发现基于CPT的学习者在面对风险敏感用户时能显著降低遗憾值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于人类偏好的奖励学习方法假设人类使用期望效用理论评估不确定结果，但行为证据表明人类决策存在风险敏感性（如低估高概率事件、高估小概率负面事件）和损失厌恶。这种不匹配会影响机器人行为对齐效果，尤其是在安全关键的社交导航场景中（如罕见碰撞事故）。

Method: 在Bradley-Terry偏好学习框架下，分别使用期望效用理论和累积前景理论建模人类偏好生成过程，通过对比两种模型在风险敏感用户偏好数据上的奖励函数恢复效果来评估其表现。

Result: 当偏好数据来自风险敏感用户时，基于CPT的奖励学习器恢复的奖励函数相比基于EU的学习器具有显著更低的遗憾值。

Conclusion: 在从随机机器人结果偏好中学习奖励时，建模人类风险敏感性至关重要。

Abstract: Learning reward functions from human preferences is a widely used approach for aligning robot behavior with user expectations in human-robot interaction. Most existing approaches assume that humans evaluate uncertain outcomes using expected utility (EU), aggregating outcome utilities linearly with their probabilities. However, behavioral evidence shows that humans are systematically risk-sensitive, overweighting rare negative events and exhibiting loss aversion. We study the consequences of this mismatch in social robot navigation, where safety-critical outcomes (e.g., collisions) are rare but highly consequential. We compare EU with Cumulative Prospect Theory (CPT), a nonlinear model of human decision-making, within a Bradley-Terry preference learning framework. Our preliminary experiments show that when preferences are generated by risk-sensitive users, CPT-based learners recover reward functions with substantially lower regret compared to EU-based learners. Our results highlight the importance of modeling human risk sensitivity when learning rewards from preferences over stochastic robot outcomes.

</details>


### [152] [Environment Design for Reliable Shared Autonomy with Probabilistic Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15487)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共享自主系统大多在固定环境下优化意图推断，忽略了工作空间设计本身对推断难度的影响。本文旨在探索环境布局作为改善共享自主系统的补充维度。

Method: 将工作空间布局形式化为优化问题，在有限噪声模型下推导概率正确性保证。通过多桌面场景的仿真实验和真实共享自主系统原型进行验证。

Result: 优化后的布局相比基线布局显著提高了目标推断可靠性并减少了歧义，在仿真和真实系统中均得到验证。

Conclusion: 环境设计是提升共享自主系统性能的有效补充维度，通过优化物理布局可以降低意图推断的难度。

Abstract: Shared autonomy enables humans and robots to collaboratively perform tasks by combining human input with autonomous assistance. Most prior work focuses on improving intent inference under a fixed environment, overlooking how workspace design itself affects inference difficulty. We observe that the physical arrangement of objects directly influences the separability of candidate goals under noisy user inputs. We formulate workspace design as an optimization problem and derive a probabilistic correctness guarantee under a bounded noise model. Through simulation experiments across multiple tabletop scenarios, we show that optimized layouts improve goal inference reliability and reduce ambiguity compared to baseline arrangements. We further demonstrate a real-world shared autonomy system that integrates the proposed inference framework. This highlights the role of environment design as a complementary axis for improving shared autonomy systems.

### [153] [Multi-Objective Kinodynamic Motion Planning with Asymptotic Pareto Optimality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15508)
*Yusif Razzaq,Anne Theurkauf,Nisar Ahmed,Morteza Lahijanian*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于SST算法的统一框架，通过在每个见证邻域维护局部Pareto最优节点集，解决了运动规划中的多目标优化问题，并给出了完备性和最优性理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的成本标量化方法无法在连续域系统中提供正确性保证，需要一种能够处理运动学约束下多目标运动规划的通用方法。

Method: 基于Stable Sparse-RRT（SST）算法，将每个见证邻域维护的单一代表节点替换为局部Pareto最优节点集，衍生出三种算法：lexSST（字典序优化）、coSST（约束优化）和poSST（Pareto前沿逼近）。

Result: 通过广泛的经验评估验证了所提算法的有效性，并提供了完备性和最优性的理论保证。

Conclusion: 提出的统一框架能够有效地解决运动学约束下的多目标运动规划三类问题，且具有理论保证。

Abstract: In this paper, we address the challenge of multi-objective motion planning for systems under kinodynamic constraints. We consider three problem classes: (i) lexicographic optimization, in which objectives are minimized according to a strict priority ordering, (ii) constrained optimization, in which a primary objective is minimized subject to bounds on the remaining costs, and (iii) Pareto front optimization, in which the goal is to approximate the full set of optimal trade-offs among competing objectives. We first show that established cost scalarization methods for multi-objective problems cannot be extended to continuous-domain systems with correctness guarantees. Then, we propose a unified algorithmic framework built upon the Stable Sparse-RRT (SST) algorithm, in which the single representative maintained at each witness neighborhood is replaced by a representative set of locally Pareto-optimal nodes. This structure gives rise to three distinct algorithms: lexSST for lexicographic minimization, coSST for constrained optimization, and poSST for Pareto-front approximation. We provide theoretical guarantees for the completeness and optimality of our algorithms and demonstrate their effectiveness through extensive empirical evaluations.

</details>

### [155] [A Model-Based Decoupling Strategy for Proprioception and Contact Sensing in an Architected Soft Manipulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15582)
*Francesco Stella,Annan Zhang,Cosimo Della Santina,Josie Hughes,Daniela Rus*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于模型驱动的策略，利用过定制的流体压力传感器系统，在软体架构化连续机器人中同时实现本体感知和接触检测。通过局部锯齿形气路通道设计和Huber回归残差分析，在单段ITH上达到弯曲误差0.11±0.02、接触检测率97%，并在多段集成的Air-Helix机械臂上演示了触觉示教、力控调节和物体重建等应用。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出Innervated Trimmed Helicoid (ITH)设计，每段含6个锯齿形气路通道；基于分段常曲率模型将压力映射为形状，利用Huber回归识别残差异常通道以检测外部接触。

Result: 单段ITH：弯曲误差0.11±0.02，178次试验中接触检测率97%。八段集成的Air-Helix实现触觉示教、力控调节和触觉物体重建。

Abstract: Soft continuum robots require embedded sensing for proprioception and contact detection, yet integrating sensors into sparse, highly deformable architected structures remains challenging. We present a model-based strategy that decouples proprioceptive and contact signals from a common set of fluidic pressure sensors embedded in a soft architected segment. Each segment of the Innervated Trimmed Helicoid (ITH) contains six air channels routed in a localized zigzag pattern along the circumference. With only three principal kinematic degrees of freedom (axial compression, bending in x, bending in y), the six pressure readings form an overdetermined system. A piecewise constant curvature model maps pressures to shape, and Huber regression identifies outlier channels whose residuals indicate external contact. On a single ITH segment, this approach achieves proprioceptive shape estimation with a relative bending error of 0.11 +/- 0.02 and a contact detection rate of 97% across 178 trials. We integrate eight ITH segments into Air-Helix, a tendon-driven soft continuum manipulator, and present exploratory whole-arm demonstrations that include tactile teaching by demonstration, admittance-controlled force regulation, and tactile object reconstruction. The results suggest that localized fluidic innervation combined with model-based redundancy resolution is a practical path toward concurrent proprioception and contact sensing in architected soft robots.

### [156] [MemoGuard: An Adaptive Runtime for Guarding Against Memory Traps in Communication-Limited Robot Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15589)
*Rajat Bhattacharjya,Hyeonjong Ju,Sing-Yao Wu,Eli Bozorgzadeh,Nikil Dutt*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出MemoGuard，一个轻量级自适应运行时系统，通过对情景记忆进行拓扑、资源和结果契约验证，在通信受限机器人任务中平衡安全性与效率。在走廊巡检模拟器和NVIDIA Jetson AGX Xavier平台上，相比纯相似度检索，电池安全违规减少76.6%；相比始终本地推理，回退调用减少21.4%，每轮节省3.67秒和36.97焦耳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通信受限的机器人在灾难巡检、搜索救援等关键任务中必须依赖机载决策，无法访问远程操作员或高容量推理服务。情景记忆复用是一种低成本回退机制，但仅靠相似度检索无法保证执行有效性（即"记忆陷阱"问题），可能导致不安全行为。现有方法在安全性与效率之间存在权衡：纯相似度复用成本低但不安全，始终调用本地推理提高安全性但计算和能耗成本高。

Method: 提出MemoGuard，一个轻量级自适应运行时系统，在复用情景记忆之前，对记忆进行三重契约验证：拓扑契约（验证环境拓扑一致性）、资源契约（验证电池等资源余量）、结果契约（验证先前执行结果的可靠性）。仅当验证通过时复用记忆，验证失败时回退到本地推理。该方法将安全验证嵌入运行时决策流程，实现自适应安全-效率权衡。

Result: 在图结构走廊巡检模拟器中，相比纯相似度top-1复用，电池安全违规减少76.6%；相比始终推理策略，回退调用减少21.4%。在NVIDIA Jetson AGX Xavier上使用llama3.2:3b作为回退推理模型，每轮实验节省3.67秒和36.97焦耳的回退推理开销。

Conclusion: MemoGuard通过轻量级契约验证机制有效解决了情景记忆复用中的"记忆陷阱"问题，在保障安全性的同时显著降低计算和能源开销，适用于资源受限的自主机器人系统。

Abstract: Communication-limited robots in mission-critical scenarios such as disaster inspection and search-and-rescue must make reliable onboard decisions without access to remote operators or high-capacity reasoning services. Episodic memory reuse is an attractive low-cost fallback, but retrieval similarity does not guarantee execution validity, i.e., a retrieved action may match the current context yet be unsafe due to changed topology, insufficient battery margin, or unreliable prior outcomes. We call such high-similarity but execution-invalid episodes memory traps. This creates a safety-efficiency design space where similarity only reuse minimizes fallback cost but can be unsafe, while always invoking local reasoning improves safety at high computational and energy cost. This paper presents MemoGuard, a lightweight adaptive runtime that validates episodic memories against topology, resource, and outcome contracts before reuse, invoking fallback only when validation fails. In a graph-based corridor-inspection simulator, MemoGuard reduces battery safety violations by 76.6% over similarity-only top-1 reuse while reducing fallback calls by 21.4% over always reasoning. On an NVIDIA Jetson AGX Xavier with local llama3.2:3b fallback reasoning, this corresponds to 3.67 s and 36.97 J of avoided fallback-reasoning overhead per trial. We open-source MemoGuard at https://github.com/hetheiin/memoguard.

</details>


### [157] [AEGIS: Assay-Aware Protocol Validation and Runtime Monitoring for Open-Source Liquid Handling Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15620)
*Priyanka V. Setty,Arvind Ramanathan,Ian Foster,Rick Stevens*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AEGIS 是一个双层守护系统，为 Opentrons OT-2 低成本液体处理器提供实验前规则验证（Layer 1，结合规则库与 LLM，F1=0.97）和运行时视觉监控（Layer 2，基于 PCA+YOLO 的移液轨迹分析，AP=0.89），统一解决操作协议错误和物理执行故障，无需付费 API，成本远低于纯 VLM 方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低成本液体处理器（如 Opentrons OT-2）缺乏高端系统（如 Hamilton、Tecan）的基于压力的吸液监测功能，通常运行在开环模式下，导致两类故障无法被检测：语法正确但违反实验特定不变量的协议（如 PCR 模板与无模板对照之间重复使用吸头），以及运行时的物理执行故障（部分分液、气泡、吸头缺失）。

Method: 双层架构：Layer 1 将人工整理的机器可读实验规则库与 LLM 配对，对 OT-2 Python 代码进行推理，在 5 个实验家族的 24 个协议基准上达到调整 F1=0.97；Layer 2 对 YOLO 裁剪的四帧移液轨迹拟合 PCA 世界模型，在无泄漏的留一板评估下达到平均精度 0.89，并结合始终运行的 VLM 自投票门控机制提升部分分液召回率。级联分流策略控制 VLM 成本。

Result: Layer 1 在五个后端上优于纯规则和纯 LLM 消融实验，开源模型与最优专有模型持平；Layer 2 在物理 OT-2 上运行（每种条件 5 个重复），确定性捕获无吸头故障，部分分液召回率提升至 5/5，透明水检测作为前端视觉的固有局限被正确处理。VLM 成本约 $1.63/板，远低于始终 VLM 基线的 $10.33/板。

Conclusion: AEGIS 是首个为开源液体处理器统一实验前协议验证与运行时视觉监测的系统，已开源。透明水等前端视觉的固有局限被系统以低置信度推理形式暴露而非错误判决，体现了设计的原则性。

Abstract: Self-driving laboratories increasingly rely on low-cost liquid handlers such as the Opentrons OT-2, which ship without the pressure-based aspiration monitoring of Hamilton or Tecan systems and are typically run open-loop. Two failure modes go undetected: protocols that are syntactically valid but violate assay-specific invariants (e.g., tip reuse between a PCR template and a no-template control), and physical execution failures (partial dispense, air bubbles, missing tips) at runtime. We present AEGIS, a two-layer guardian for both. Layer 1 pairs a curated machine-readable assay rule database with an LLM that reasons over OT-2 Python code, reaching an adjusted F1 of 0.97 on a 24-protocol benchmark across five assay families and beating rules-only and LLM-only ablations across five backends; a free open-weight model ties the best proprietary one, so no paid API is required. Layer 2 fits a PCA world model to YOLO-cropped four-frame pipette trajectories; under a leakage-free leave-one-plate-out evaluation it reaches average precision 0.89 and operating-point F1 0.71 (AUROC 0.80), a deployment-faithful number that matches the live demonstration, and we characterize the small-pipette (p20) resolution limit (F1 0.47). A live demonstration on a physical OT-2 (five replicates per condition) catches planted no-tip failures deterministically and partial dispense on coloured dyes, with an always-VLM self-vote gate lifting partial-dispense recall to 5/5; transparent water is a principled limit of any front-view-only monitor, which AEGIS surfaces as low-confidence VLM reasoning rather than a wrong verdict. Cascade triage holds VLM cost near $1.63 per plate versus $10.33 for an always-VLM baseline. AEGIS is open source and, to our knowledge, the first system to unify pre-flight assay-aware validation with runtime visual monitoring for an open-source liquid handler.

### [158] [Think at 5 Hz, Act at 20 Hz: Asynchronous Fast-Slow Vision-Language-Action Inference for Closed-Loop Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15621)
*Yun Li,Jiachen Gong,Simon Thompson,Ehsan Javanmardi,Qunli Zhang,Zifan Zeng,Shiming Liu,Peng Wang,Zixuan Guo,Manabu Tsukada*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出一种快慢双架构的端到端驾驶系统，使用冻结的7B视觉语言模型作为慢系统（低频处理导航指令和视觉历史），轻量级动作专家作为快系统（每个仿真tick实时预测航点），通过随机延迟训练对齐异步执行，在CARLA上实现94.0的路线完成率，比跳帧基线提升57个百分点，单个GPU上每tick仅需32ms。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在端到端驾驶中具备指令跟随和场景推理能力，但其推理延迟与车辆控制频率存在冲突。现有方案通过跳帧（每两个仿真tick调用一次模型，中间重复上一个指令）来弥补这一差距，导致半数控制输出忽略最新观测，严重影响安全性和驾驶性能。

Method: 1) 快慢架构：冻结的7B视觉语言模型（慢系统）低频处理导航指令和视觉历史，暴露每层KV缓存作为场景表示；轻量级动作专家（快系统）每个仿真tick关注该缓存和当前相机帧，单次前向传播回归航点。2) 随机延迟训练：在训练时引入随机滞后的KV缓存，使专家适应部署时的异步执行延迟。

Result: LangAuto-Short路线上，路线完成率从37.0提升至94.0，每个50ms仿真tick均产生新控制信号。跳帧消融实验表明：专家本身提升驾驶分数，而逐tick的新鲜度将完成率从82.1提升至94.0，并减少三分之一的闯红灯违规。在单一城镇训练后零样本迁移至两个未见城镇，完成率保持84-94%（基线31-41%）。开放环航点误差相比骨干网络自身动作头降低近4倍，单tick模型开销32ms（与历史长度无关）。

Conclusion: 快慢架构有效解决了LLM推理延迟与驾驶控制频率的矛盾，在保持大模型场景理解能力的同时实现了实时控制输出，且具备良好的零样本迁移能力。

Abstract: Large language models bring instruction following and scene reasoning to end-to-end driving, but their inference latency collides with the control rate a vehicle requires. Existing closed-loop agents hide this gap by invoking the model on alternate simulation ticks and replaying the previous command in between, so half of all control outputs ignore the newest observations. We present a fast-slow architecture that removes this compromise. A frozen 7B vision-language backbone acts as the slow system, digesting navigation instructions and visual history at low frequency while exposing its per-layer key-value cache as a standing representation of the scene. A lightweight action expert acts as the fast system, attending to this cache and to the current camera frame at every simulation tick to regress waypoints in a single forward pass. Since the cache lags behind the world at deployment, we train the expert under randomized staleness, aligning training with asynchronous execution. On LangAuto-Short routes in CARLA, our system produces fresh control at every 50 ms simulation tick and lifts route completion from 37.0 to 94.0 over the frame-skipping baseline. A frame-skip ablation with the same expert separates the two factors at work: the expert raises the driving score on its own, while per-tick freshness raises completion from 82.1 to 94.0 and cuts red-light violations by a third. Trained on a single town, the expert transfers zero-shot to two unseen towns, holding 84-94% route completion where the baseline reaches 31-41%. It reduces open-loop waypoint error by nearly a factor of four compared to the backbone's own action head, at a per-tick model cost of 32 ms that is independent of history length on a single consumer GPU.

### [160] [IMBench: A Benchmark for Intuitive Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15641)
*Anurag Maurya,Sukhvansh Jain,Prajwal Avhad,Gautham Balachandran,Ziyi Zhou,Atharva Kshirsagar,Satyam Singh,Bowen Li. Rishabh Mukund,Ritul Singh,Jatin Vira,Suvonil Chatterjee,Devesh K. Jha*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了IMBENCH基准，用于评估机器人直觉操作能力（整合物理推理与动作执行），发现现有视觉语言模型和视觉-语言-动作模型均无法有效结合推理与执行，揭示了当前基础模型在物理智能上的缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准要么孤立评估物理推理而不涉及执行，要么只测量策略性能而不要求显式推理，无法捕捉人类将推理与运动控制结合的直觉操作能力，因此需要一个新的基准来综合评估这种整合能力。

Method: 构建了包含35个任务、14K过滤轨迹的IMBENCH基准，涵盖接触丰富的操作、工具使用和多阶段依赖等场景，并设计了可扩展的场景生成工具。

Conclusion: 直觉操作是当前基础模型和通用机器人策略中缺失的关键维度，IMBENCH可作为评估和推动更整合的自适应物理智能的重要步骤。

Abstract: Humans combine reasoning and motor control to solve complex manipulation tasks under diverse constraints. They build an understanding of the physical world that helps them convert reasoning into actions and quickly adapt to new scenes, tasks, and rules. We refer to this capability as intuitive manipulation. Existing benchmarks fail to capture this integration: they evaluate physical reasoning in isolation from execution, or measure policy performance without requiring explicit reasoning. We introduce IMBENCH, a benchmark designed to evaluate intuitive manipulation as an integrated capability spanning perception, physical reasoning, action generation, and iterative execution. Our tasks require models to infer task-relevant physical structure and generate feasible action sequences under explicit constraints, including contact-rich manipulation, tool use, and multi-stage dependencies. We introduce a benchmark of 35 tasks, 14K filtered trajectories, and scalable tools for generating diverse scenarios. Experiments reveal a consistent gap: vision language models show partial physical reasoning ability but fail to produce executable plans, while state-of-the-art vision-language-action models struggle to satisfy task constraints and generalize across scenarios. These results identify intuitive manipulation as a missing axis in current foundation models and generalist robot policies, and position IMBENCH as a step toward evaluating and enabling more integrated, adaptive physical intelligence.

*Guolei Qi,Feitian Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文提出T-DRN网络，通过孪生差分特征提取器和双帧时序缓冲区，实现零样本的sim-to-real物体目标视觉导航，在AI2-THOR仿真和实体机器人上均取得优于基线方法的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出时序差分关系网络（T-DRN），包含两个关键模块：1）孪生差分特征提取器，计算目标与观测物体之间的关系差分，生成域无关的特征表示；2）双帧时序缓冲区，在窄FoV下保持短期物体的连续性。

Conclusion: T-DRN通过域无关的差分特征表示和时序信息保持，有效弥合了仿真到现实的差距，实现了零样本的物体目标视觉导航，具备在实际机器人平台上部署的潜力。

Abstract: End-to-end deep reinforcement learning (DRL) for zero-shot object-goal visual navigation remains challenged by the sim-to-real gap, particularly variations in object appearance and restricted camera field-of-view (FoV). This letter proposes a Temporal Difference-Relational Network (T-DRN) for robust zero-shot sim-to-real transfer. T-DRN combines a Siamese difference-based feature extractor, which computes relational difference between the target and observed objects to produce domain-independent representations, with a dual-frame temporal buffer that preserves short-term object continuity under narrow FoV. Extensive experiments in AI2-THOR demonstrate that T-DRN improves zero-shot generalization in terms of success rates over strong baselines. Furthermore, T-DRN is systematically validated on a physical wheeled robot, demonstrating robust performance under real sensing and actuation constraints and supporting the feasibility of direct sim-to-real transfer.

In this study, we present a continuously stable structure through plastic deformation (CSSPD), integrated into a soft gripper. We introduce a bioinspired paw pad that significantly enhances stability and enables sensing-based rapid object grasping. ### [164] [A Generative Partially Specified Finite State Machine Approach to Complex Behaviour Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15674)
*Kalana Ratnayake,Michael Pritchard,David Hinwood,Maleen Jayasuriya,Damith Herath*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种生成式部分指定有限状态机（GPSFSM）神经符号架构，结合FSM的符号语义结构与LLM的生成能力，用于机器人行为规划。实验表明该方法在导航任务中实现了比现有BTGenBot系统更高的一致计划生成成功率，尤其在零样本场景中表现优异，并开源了完整的ROS2实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出GPSFSM神经符号架构，包含三个核心组件：1) Fabric——FSM引擎，解析、验证并执行包含顺序、恢复、并行任意和并行全部四种控制结构的行为计划；2) 扩展Capabilities2包，引入异步事件系统用于行为链式调用和运行时参数注入；3) PromptTools——统一的ROS2接口，支持本地和云端LLM的提示缓冲，实现任务和上下文信息的动态异步组合。系统利用FSM的状态和事件触发转换的符号语义结构来实现行为规划。

Conclusion: 首次将生成式FSM框架引入机器人领域，通过标准化语义能力描述实现机器人无关开发，并开源ROS2栈使生成式FSM规划实用且可复现，为机器人行为规划提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Autonomous robots operating in dynamic environments require behaviour planning systems that combine reactivity, interpretability, and adaptability. While Large Language Models have been successfully integrated with Behaviour Trees for dynamic replanning, Finite State Machines, despite their widespread adoption and computational efficiency, remain unexplored for generative approaches. We propose a Generative Partially Specified Finite State Machine (GPSFSM) neurosymbolic architecture that utilises the symbolic and semantic structure of FSMs, including states and event-triggered transitions, to implement Behaviour Planning. This paper introduces the first GPSFSM framework for robotics, featuring Fabric, an FSM engine that parses, validates, and executes behaviour plans that contain Sequential, Recovery, Parallel-Any, and Parallel-All control structures. We extend the Capabilities2 package in ROS2 with an asynchronous event system for behaviour chaining and runtime parameter injection for configurable execution, addressing the ad-hoc function representations that limit current generative systems. PromptTools provides a unified ROS 2 interface to local and cloud LLMs, with prompt buffering, enabling dynamic asynchronous composition of task and context information. Together, these components enable standardised semantic capability descriptions for robot-agnostic development. Experimental evaluation on navigation tasks demonstrates that our GPSFSM approach achieves consistently higher plan-generation success rates than the state-of-the-art BTGenBot system, particularly excelling in zero-shot scenarios where BTs typically struggle, while maintaining comparable or lower planning latency to frontier LLMs. We also demonstrate that our system can generate complex behaviours. We release an open-source ROS2 stack that makes generative FSM planning practical and reproducible for robotic systems.

### [165] [RAVEN: Reinforcement-Adaptive Visibility-Graph Planning for Robust Humanoid Navigation with Collision-Free MPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15701)
*Ruochen Hou,Shiqi Wang,Beom Jun Kim,Hanzhang Fang,Mehak Singal,Dennis W. Hong*

Main category: cs.RO

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统可见性图-MPC方法依赖手动调参和精确系统建模，在存在控制延迟、状态估计噪声和 locomotion 不确定性的实际机器人系统中，即使名义路径几何最优也会出现过冲和约束违反。

Method: 提出RAVEN层次化强化学习-MPC框架：上层RL通过修改障碍物膨胀和相关图参数来调整可见性图规划器的几何构建，重塑自由空间拓扑以补偿延迟和跟踪缺陷；下层碰撞-free MPC跟踪规划轨迹并显式强制执行速度界限和避障约束。在真实延迟和观测噪声下训练。

Abstract: Humanoid navigation in dynamic environments requires long-horizon planning while respecting short-horizon dynamic and safety constraints. Classical visibility-graph planners combined with model predictive control (MPC) can efficiently generate collision-free trajectories, but their performance depends on manually tuned parameters and accurate system modeling. In real robotic systems, control delays, state-estimation noise, and locomotion uncertainties can cause overshoot and constraint violations even when the nominal path is geometrically optimal. We propose RAVEN, a hierarchical reinforcement learning (RL)-MPC framework for robust humanoid navigation. Unlike prior approaches that use learning to tune cost weights or replace planning entirely, RAVEN employs RL to adapt the geometric construction of a visibility-graph planner by modifying obstacle inflation and related graph parameters. By directly reshaping the free-space geometry, the learned planner alters the topology of the global path to compensate for delay and tracking imperfections. A collision-free MPC layer then tracks the planned trajectory while explicitly enforcing velocity bounds and obstacle-avoidance constraints. By training under realistic delays and observation noise, RAVEN learns planning adaptations that improve robustness while retaining explicit long-horizon geometric planning and constrained optimization, in contrast to end-to-end learning approaches. We evaluate RAVEN against a manually tuned visibility-graph MPC baseline and a pure RL navigation policy. Results demonstrate reduced overshoot near obstacles, improved robustness in narrow passages, and more reliable navigation under delay and noise. These findings indicate that reinforcement-adaptive graph construction combined with constrained MPC provides an effective and interpretable alternative to end-to-end learning for robust humanoid navigation.

### [167] [AC-VLA: Robust Out-of-Distribution Action Execution via Compositional Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15714)
*Xiaojiang Peng,Kai Peng,Jie Lu,Zheng Lian,Zitong YU,Xiaobo Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: AC-VLA提出了一种即插即用的动作组合学习框架，通过LLM驱动的指令分解器、本体轨迹对齐器生成密集子任务监督，并结合状态条件非对称掩码策略，解决VLA模型在组合泛化中的轨迹过拟合和感知捷径问题，在LIBERO-OOD基准上实现约28%的绝对提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型在端到端机器人操作中表现出色，但当熟悉子任务以未见配置重新组合时，面临分布外泛化困难。论文识别出两个相互强化的失败模式：轨迹过拟合（模型过度拟合整体轨迹模式而非组合性子技能语义）和感知捷径（动作标记过度依赖腕部视角纹理而忽略全局空间定位）。

Method: 提出AC-VLA框架，包含两个架构无关组件：(1) 组合学习模块，使用LLM驱动的指令分解器和本体轨迹对齐器生成密集子任务监督，并通过完整演示与分解数据的混合训练赋予模型组合泛化能力；(2) 状态条件非对称掩码策略，在夹爪闭合阶段抑制腕部视角输入，强制模型学习全局语义定位。所有组件无需修改架构即可集成到任何VLA骨干网络中。

Conclusion: AC-VLA通过即插即用的方式有效解决了VLA模型在组合泛化中的两大核心问题，且无需修改模型架构即可集成到现有VLA骨干中，在显著提升OOD泛化能力的同时不牺牲分布内性能。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models excel at end-to-end robotic manipulation but struggle with out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization when familiar sub-tasks are recombined in unseen configurations. We identify two mutually reinforcing failure modes: \emph{trajectory overfitting}, where models overfit to holistic trajectory patterns rather than compositional sub-skill semantics; and \emph{perceptual shortcut}, where action tokens over-rely on wrist-view textures at the expense of global spatial grounding. To address both, we introduce \textbf{AC-VLA}, a plug-and-play Action Compositional learning framework comprising two architecture-agnostic components: \textbf{(i)} a compositional learning module that uses an LLM-driven instruction decomposer and a proprioceptive trajectory aligner to generate dense sub-task supervision, followed by mixed training on complete demonstrations and decomposed data to endow the model with compositional generalization; and \textbf{(ii)} a state-conditioned asymmetric masking strategy that suppresses wrist-view inputs during closed-gripper phases, enforcing global semantic grounding. All components are architectural modification-free and directly integrable into any VLA backbone. Instantiated on $π_{0.5}$ and evaluated on LIBERO and LIBERO-OOD benchmarks, AC-VLA achieves a ~28% absolute improvement on compositional OOD tasks while maintaining near-perfect in-distribution performance.

### [168] [A Task-Space Receding Horizon Controller for Fast Collision Avoidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15733)
*Mattia Penzotti,Marco Controzzi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全模型预测控制（MPC）能提供前瞻能力，但随预测时域、模型精度和几何约束数量增加，在线计算成本快速增长；而无时域的反应式方法计算高效，但在动态杂乱环境中视野短浅、容易陷入困境。需要一种兼顾前瞻性与实时性的方法。

Method: 1) 采用任务空间滚动时域控制框架，通过短时接触一致滚动（contact-consistent rollout）生成满足内部非穿透约束的终端运动学参考；2) 仅计算朝向该参考的平滑最小加速度过渡的第一个输入；3) 滚动过程基于闭链逆运动学（CLIK）调节律，使用迭代动力学求解器处理膨胀的凸机器人/障碍物几何，使机器人-障碍物接触、动态障碍物运动及自碰撞均可塑造终端参考，无需完整约束轨迹优化；4) 对接触非激活闭环进行局部指数稳定分析，对接触激活情况刻画离散更新并界定移动障碍物对正则工作集的影响。

Result: 40自由度多链系统仿真表明中等时域可平衡预测性、响应性与计算成本；6自由度平台硬件实验展示出一致的仿真到真实迁移行为，无需精确惯性参数估计；与动态优化织物和MPC基线的对比显示，在动态杂乱环境中成功率更高，同时保持实时可执行的求解时间。

Conclusion: 该控制器通过短时滚动与接触一致生成，在计算效率与前瞻能力之间取得了有效平衡，在动态环境中优于基线方法，且具有良好的仿真到真实迁移性。

Abstract: Real-time collision avoidance for robotic manipulators requires fast reactions to unexpected obstacle motion and lookahead to avoid becoming trapped by near-future constraints. Full model predictive control can provide this foresight, but its online cost may grow quickly with horizon length, model fidelity, and the number of active geometric constraints. Conversely, horizon-free reactive methods are computationally efficient but can be short-sighted in dynamic clutter. We present a task-space receding-horizon controller that uses a short contact-consistent rollout to generate a terminal kinematic reference satisfying internal non-penetration constraints, then computes only the first input of a smooth minimum-acceleration transition toward that reference. Starting from a closed-loop inverse-kinematics regulation law, the rollout is performed with an iterative dynamics solver operating on inflated convex robot and obstacle geometries, so that robot-obstacle contacts, dynamic obstacle motion, and self-collisions can shape the terminal reference without requiring full constrained trajectory optimization. We analyze the contact-inactive closed loop and show local exponential task-space regulation under standard regularity assumptions. For contacts activated inside the rollout, we characterize the corresponding discrete updates and bound the effect of moving obstacles on regular operating sets. Simulations on a 40-DOF multi-chain system show that intermediate horizons balance anticipation, responsiveness, and computational cost. Hardware experiments on a 6-DOF platform demonstrate consistent sim-to-real behavior without accurate inertial parameter estimation, and comparisons against dynamic optimization fabrics and model predictive control (MPC) baselines show improved success rates in dynamic clutter while preserving solve times compatible with real-time execution in the tested regimes.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人系统需要接近人类皮肤适应性和分辨率的触觉传感能力，以实现灵巧操作和安全交互，但现有触觉传感器在空间分辨率与信号传输方面存在局限。

Method: 采用仿生设计，将柔性皮肤上的每个机械针与光纤（人工神经）配对，模拟生物触觉的机械感受器-神经架构；将触觉信号视为图像，使用简单解析方法而非深度学习模型推断接触位置、大小和形状。

Result: 实现了触觉信息从传感表面的有效路由，同时保留了高空间分辨率；通过可解释的解析方法准确推断接触位置、大小和形状，避免了深度学习的黑箱问题。

Conclusion: OptiTac建立了人工神经启发的触觉传感框架，为机器人提供可解释的触觉智能，并为未来分布式触觉系统提供可扩展的技术路径，展示了生物学进化原理在机器人人工神经系统中应用的可行性。

Abstract: Robotic systems increasingly demand tactile sensing that approaches the adaptability and resolution of human skin to enable dexterous manipulation and safe interaction. OptiTac is a biomimetic tactile sensor that emulates the mechanoreceptor-to-nerve architecture of human touch by pairing each mechanical pin on a soft skin with an optical fiber acting as an artificial nerve. This design demonstrates an architectural principle for routing tactile information away from the sensing surface while preserving high spatial resolution, establishing a practical route toward distributed tactile sensing in future robotic systems. By treating tactile signals as images, simple analytical methods, rather than opaque deep-learning models, are used to infer contact location, size, and shape, providing interpretable and scalable tactile intelligence. This work demonstrates how evolutionary principles from biology can guide the development of artificial nerve systems for robots, offering a pathway toward human-like tactile perception in next-generation robotic platforms. More broadly, OptiTac establishes an artificial nerve-inspired sensing framework for interpretable robotic touch and a scalable route toward future distributed tactile systems.

### [170] [SkillNav: Score-Level Skill Intervention for Zero-Shot Object Goal Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15758)
*Ruijie Sang,Yiqun Duan,Pinhan Fu,Ruilin Wang,Wei Sui,Xianda Guo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: SkillNav提出了一种可扩展的行为技能框架，通过在已有的好奇值地图上以零Token成本写入行为记忆，解决VLM导航代理因缺乏跨步行为意识导致的死胡同、室内循环等问题。技能分为三级（软缩放、下限提升、硬覆盖），按固定优先级协作，新行为通过注册即可加入而无须重新训练。该方法在MP3D、HM3D上取得新SOTA SPL，分别提升最多6.0绝对值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM导航代理依赖单帧推理，缺乏跨步行为意识，导致死胡同、室内循环、迂回接近目标等重复失败。基于提示的补救方法会膨胀多子模块的Token预算，且难以编码角度、地图单元、视角坐标等空间信号。

Method: 提出SkillNav框架：将VLM导航器已有的好奇值地图作为可写基板，技能以零Token成本在地图上刻写行为记忆。技能分为三级——软缩放（比例重加权）、下限提升（区域级保证）、硬覆盖（阈值触发强制动作），按固定组合顺序协作。新行为通过注册接入，无须重训练VLM或干扰现有技能。额外使用极简提示通道提供类别级语义提示，形成"空间记忆在地图、语义记忆在短提示"的双重表征设计。

Result: 在MP3D上SPL达25.5，HM3D v0.1上SPL 39.3、SR 69.7，HM3D v0.2上SPL 43.2、SR 75.9，均超越先前最强方法，SPL提升最高达6.0绝对值。

Conclusion: SkillNav是训练免费、可扩展的行为技能框架，通过将能力改进转化为技能注册，为持续优化开辟路径，在零样本目标导航任务上建立了新SOTA。

Abstract: Vision-Language Model (VLM) agents have advanced zero-shot object-goal navigation, yet single-frame reasoning leaves them without the cross-step behavioral awareness an embodied navigator requires, producing recurring failures such as dead-end stalls, in-room loops, and circuitous approaches to detected targets. Prompt-based remedies inflate token budgets across multi-submodule episodes and still struggle to encode inherently spatial signals such as angles, map cells, and viewpoint coordinates. In this paper, we propose SkillNav, an extensible behavioral skill framework for VLM-based navigation that treats the curiosity value map already maintained by modern VLM navigators as a writable substrate on which composable skills inscribe behavioral memory at zero token cost. Skills are stratified into three tiers by their level of behavioral authority, namely soft scaling for proportional reweighting, lower-bound boost for region-level guarantees, and hard override for threshold-triggered forced actions, and cooperate across tiers under a fixed composition order that establishes a predictable, declared priority among skills. This design turns capability improvement into skill registration: new behaviors plug in without retraining the VLM or disturbing existing skills, opening a path for continual refinement. A minimal prompt channel complements the score-level skills with category-level semantic hints, yielding a dual-representation design in which spatial memory lives on the map and semantic memory in short prompts. Training-free, SkillNav establishes new state-of-the-art SPL across MP3D (25.5), HM3D v0.1 (39.3), and HM3D v0.2 (43.2), improving SPL by up to 6.0 absolute over the strongest prior method, and achieves the highest Success Rate on HM3D v0.1 (69.7) and v0.2 (75.9).

Abstract: Ultra-Wideband (UWB) ranging has become a viable option for industrial Autonomous Mobile Robot (AMR) localization due to improved accuracy and low cost. However, real-world deployments remain limited by two recurring challenges: calibrating static anchors can be time-consuming and error-prone, and integrating UWB with existing onboard sensors requires careful design to ensure robust and consistent pose estimation. Addressing these challenges, this paper presents an end-to-end pipeline that combines automatic anchor calibration with a generic multi-sensor estimator tailored to surface-bound vehicle motion. It targets existing AMR stacks in scenarios where robot pose priors are available for initialization. The calibration stage estimates anchor positions and range biases, while the localization stage fuses UWB with proprioceptive sensing in a bias-aware Extended Kalman Filter to improve consistency without extensive parameter tuning. Experiments on a commercial logistics AMR in a warehouse setting demonstrate accurate positioning indoors and across outdoor transitions, with improved consistency compared to an earlier estimator formulation. Evaluation on an independent forklift dataset further indicates transferability to other platforms. The method remains effective in test cases with limited line-of-sight and sparse anchor coverage. These results show that UWB localization can be deployed with substantially reduced manual effort while preserving the accuracy required for industrial AMRs. The collected warehouse dataset is made publicly available.

### [172] [Beyond Frontiers: Scene-Anomaly Guided Autonomous Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15828)

TL;DR: 本文提出SCAGE框架，将自主3D探索重新定义为几何异常最小化问题。与传统的基于覆盖最大化的启发式方法不同，SCAGE利用对标准室内建筑的基础理解，将实时3D观测与学习到的先验知识进行对比，将不一致区域（如破碎的墙壁、不完整的桌子）标记为场景异常，并引导机器人从最优视角主动调查和解决这些结构异常，从而同时实现空间覆盖与高质量重建。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出SCAGE框架，直接在非结构化的3D点云上运行。机器人具备对标准室内建筑的基础理解，在导航过程中持续将实时3D观测与学习到的先验期望进行对比；当传入几何与先验矛盾时（如破碎的墙壁、不完整的桌子），系统将这些区域标记为场景异常，并以此为引导信号，驱动机器人从最优视角调查和解决这些结构异常。

Conclusion: 通过主动定位重建质量差的区域而非仅仅探索空白空间，SCAGE将空间发现与高保真建图无缝耦合，实现了高效探索与高质量重建的统一。

Abstract: Autonomous exploration of unknown 3D environments is traditionally driven by coverage-maximizing geometric heuristics. However, these methods typically determine exploration targets without considering the underlying structural context. This leads to inefficient trajectories often limiting the fidelity of the final 3D reconstruction. To bridge the gap between spatial coverage and reconstruction quality, we introduce a novel paradigm: reframing exploration as a geometric anomaly minimization problem. We present SCAGE: SCene Anomaly Guided Exploration, a novel autonomous exploration framework that operates directly on unstructured 3D point clouds. Instead of blindly chasing volumetric boundaries, we equip the robot with a foundational understanding of standard indoor architecture. As the robot navigates, it continuously evaluates its live 3D observations against these learned expectations. When the incoming geometry contradicts the learned priors of a typical indoor environment, such as a fragmented wall or a partial table, the system flags these regions as scene anomalies. These geometric inconsistencies act as a guiding signal, naturally drawing the robot to investigate and resolve these structural anomalies from optimal vantage points. By actively targeting poorly reconstructed regions rather than just empty space, our approach seamlessly couples spatial discovery with high-fidelity mapping. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that SCAGE achieves superior volumetric coverage (~90% in all scenes) and higher 3D reconstruction quality compared to state-of-the-art baselines.

We introduce the Visual-Motor Trajectory (VMT) module to capture complex spatio-temporal dynamics within the task latent space. Furthermore, we propose the Unpaired Unified Task (U2T) block to fuse unstructured multimodal observations. To coordinate these representations, we integrate a Task-Conditioned Feature Modulation (TCFM) mechanism customized for modulating low-level 3D features. By capturing intrinsic dynamics from a random complete reference demonstration, our framework learns the underlying task logic rather than memorizing static cues, ensuring effective generalization. *Hadrien Crassous,Mohamed Yassine Kabouri,Minahil Raza,Joni Pajarinen,Riad Akrour*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在机器人导航时间和标注预算双重约束下，通过空间一致性引导的具身主动学习策略，使计算机视觉目标检测器能够适应未知环境。该方法在每个轮次中，智能体利用有限的导航预算收集候选样本，再以有限的标注预算选择最相关的图像进行重训练，通过识别标签不一致的图像（这些图像最可能提升视觉模型性能）来显式针对检测器的失败案例进行优化。在AI2-THOR模拟器和波士顿动力Spot机器人+ YOLOv5的实际场景中，该方法在相同预算下相比多种基线达到了最高的检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人部署到未知环境时，目标检测器性能会因分布偏移而显著下降，而重新收集和标注大量训练数据既昂贵又耗时。如何在有限的导航时间（机器人自主探索代价）和有限的标注预算（人工标注代价）双重约束下，高效地适应目标检测器是一个关键挑战。

Method: 提出了具身批量主动学习框架：每一轮智能体在导航预算内沿轨迹采集候选图像，然后利用**空间一致性**（即同一场景中不同视角下对同一物体的检测标签是否一致）来识别标签不一致的失败案例图像，这些图像被优先送至人工标注并加入训练集对检测器进行重训练。该方法不需要外部监督信号，完全依靠检测器自身输出的空间不一致性来引导采样。

Result: 在AI2-THOR模拟器的大规模场景以及波士顿动力Spot机器人搭载YOLOv5的真实环境中，该方法在相同的导航和标注预算下，最终检测精度均优于多种基线方法（如随机采样、不确定性采样等），证明了空间一致性能有效引导智能体选择最有价值的图像进行标注。

Conclusion: 空间不一致性是一种无需外部监督的有效信号，能够在具身主动学习的预算约束下，帮助智能体自主定位并选择目标检测器的失败案例，从而在有限资源下实现最高效的模型适应。

Abstract: This paper studies how to adapt a computer vision object detector to an unknown environment under both a robot navigation time and annotation budget constraint. Our approach selects informative robot trajectories and image samples to retrain the detector, explicitly targeting its failure cases. Formally, the approach is an embodied variant of batch active learning, where at each round an agent has a limited navigation budget to collect candidate samples and a limited annotation budget for the most relevant images. We leverage spatial consistency to identify images with inconsistent labels, which are likely to provide the greatest improvement to the vision model. We evaluate the approach using different active learning objectives on large scenes from the AI2-THOR simulator and on a real-world setup using a Boston Dynamics Spot robot with the real-time object detector YOLOv5. Through comparison against several baselines, our experimental results show that spatial inconsistency helps guide the agent and select relevant images without external supervision, achieving the highest detection accuracy at the end of the adaptation process under the same budget. The open-source project can be found at https://mkabouri.github.io/embodied-active-learning-od

</details>


### [177] [Data and Learning Where it Matters for Contact-Rich Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15982)
*Oliver Hausdörfer,Linus Schwarz,Gabor Marko,Christian Dietz,Timo Class,Luka Hofer,Jim Yun-Jin Li,Johannes Hechtl,Ralf Römer,Angela P. Schoellig*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对接触密集型任务的自动化数据收集方案，结合离线深度强化学习，仅用2-2.5小时自主数据收集即在四个真实世界任务中达到96%平均成功率，远超基线方法的55%，并在分布外场景中保持高性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 端到端学习策略在高精度任务中仍然脆弱且泛化能力差，主要原因在于数据收集缺乏结构和重点。

Method: 仅在接触密集型任务的关键段进行密集数据收集，自由空间运动依赖传统规划；采用自动化数据收集方案结合离线深度强化学习，无需远程操作员技能和在线策略更新。

Result: 在四个真实世界任务中，2-2.5小时自主数据收集实现平均96%成功率（最强基线55%），且在分布外场景中表现优异。

Abstract: Learned policies trained end-to-end on large datasets often remain brittle in high-precision tasks and struggle with generalization. We find that these limitations largely stem from a lack of structure and focus in data collection. Our key insight is to leverage dense data collection only for the critical segment of contact-rich tasks and to rely on traditional planning during simple free-space motion. We propose an automated data-collection scheme in combination with offline deep reinforcement learning for the critical segment of the task, eliminating reliance on a teleoperator's skill and on online policy updates. Across four challenging real-world tasks, using only 2 to 2.5 hours of autonomous data collection, we achieve an average success rate of 96%, compared to the strongest baseline at 55%. Notably, performance remains high in out-of-distribution scenarios where end-to-end approaches struggle. Our results pave the way for targeted data collection for contact-rich tasks and for high success rates in precision applications.

<details>

Method: 使用开源变形平台，连续改变相邻螺旋桨夹角，构建不同几何构型；通过数据拟合的经验功耗模型评估效率，通过定位精度和旋转动能评估故障状态下的实际弹性；实验验证几何可行区域的存在性。

Conclusion: Opti-Hexa原型机在相同尺寸、重量、硬件和软件条件下，实现了抗单桨故障弹性与能效的兼顾；开源发布完整软硬件以支持后续研究。

Abstract: This work demonstrates experimentally the existence of a hexarotor prototype, termed Opti-Hexa, that simultaneously achieves practical resilience to single-propeller failures and energy efficiency comparable to a standard Star-shaped prototype with the same size, weight, hardware and software. Leveraging a novel open-source morphing platform, we investigate the trade-offs across a continuous range of geometries by varying the angles between adjacent propellers. We study practical efficiency through a data-fitted empirical power model and evaluate practical resilience by comparing the position accuracy and rotational kinetic energy during failure to those observed under nominal hovering conditions. Our experiments confirm the existence of a geometric viability region for this specific morphing platform, where resilience is ensured without the aerodynamic efficiency losses typically associated with practically resilient designs found in the state of the art. The complete hardware and software of the morphing platform are released to support further research.

### [179] [Let the Body Follow: Coupled Egocentric Control for Whole-Body Robot Teleoperation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16095)
*Tsung-Chi Lin,Yichen Xie,Chien-Ming Huang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出耦合自我中心控制（coupled egocentric control），让机器人躯干和底座自动跟随操作者头部和手臂运动，无需手动指令。在TIAGo移动机械臂的全身体感遥控用户研究中，相比混合基线界面，该方法提高了操作效率，减少了按钮控制负担和手臂奇异点，降低了脑力负荷，提升了易用性和用户偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全身遥操作需要用户同时协调机器人头部、手臂、躯干和底座的运动，同时保持任务感知并避免运动学和环境约束，这对用户造成巨大的操作负担。

Method: 提出耦合自我中心控制方法：头部俯仰调节躯干高度，头部偏航驱动底座旋转，末端执行器高度调节躯干运动，末端执行器工作空间边界触发底座平移。

Result: 相比混合基线界面，耦合自我中心控制提升了物体操作效率，减少了按钮控制负担和手臂奇异点，降低了脑力需求和整体工作负荷，提高了易用性、易学性、信心以及用户对躯干和底座控制的偏好。

Conclusion: 耦合自我中心控制能有效简化全身遥操作，让用户专注于视线和手部控制，自动处理躯干和底座的协调运动，从而降低操作复杂度和认知负荷。

Abstract: Whole-body teleoperation requires users to coordinate perception, manipulation, posture, and mobility across multiple robot components. This coordination is difficult because users must simultaneously control the robot's head, arms, torso, and base while maintaining task awareness and avoiding kinematic or environmental constraints. In this paper, we propose coupled egocentric control, a body-following teleoperation approach in which the robot's torso and base automatically respond to the operator's head and arm motions. Rather than requiring explicit touchpad commands for every torso or base adjustment, the system lets users focus on gaze and hand control: head pitch adjusts torso height, head yaw drives base rotation, end-effector height adjusts torso motion, and end-effector workspace boundaries trigger base translation. We evaluate this approach in a user study on whole-body teleoperation of a TIAGo mobile manipulator for home-care-inspired tasks. Compared with a baseline hybrid interface, coupled egocentric control improves object manipulation efficiency, reduces button-based control effort and arm singularities, lowers mental demand and overall workload, and increases ease of use, ease of learning, confidence, and user preference for torso and base control.

### [180] [BayesContact: Uncertain Pose Estimation via Visuo-Tactile Proposals and Simulation-based Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16123)
*Aditya Kamireddypalli,Matias Mattamala,Joao Moura,Russell Buchanan,Sethu Vijayakumar,Subramanian Ramamoorthy*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出BayesContact，一种基于模拟推理的视觉-触觉位姿估计框架，用于轴孔插入任务。通过粒子滤波融合深度观测和力/触觉接触证据，利用渲染器和物理模拟器分别预测深度和接触结果，多模态信念还能用于主动探索歧义区域。在仿真和实际实验中，相比纯视觉方法，位姿可观测性和插入成功率提升30%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 接触丰富的操作任务需要比纯深度感知更精确的位姿估计，而现有依赖视觉和接触的方法需要昂贵的离线训练，且对新的环境和几何结构需要重新训练，泛化性差。

Method: 采用基于模拟推理的框架BayesContact：维护物体位姿的粒子信念，融合深度观测和力/力矩触接触证据；利用渲染器预测每个位姿假设下的深度测量，物理模拟器预测探测动作下的接触结果；通过对比真实观测更新信念，并利用信息增益指导主动探索。

Result: 在多种仿真几何体和真实机器人实验中，相比纯视觉推理，BayesContact的位姿可观测性和插入成功率提升30%。

Conclusion: BayesContact通过模拟推理有效融合视觉和触觉信息，避免了昂贵的数据收集和重新训练，提升了接触丰富操作任务的位姿估计精度和任务成功率。

Abstract: Contact-rich manipulation requires pose estimates that are often more accurate than what depth-only sensing provides. Existing methods, relying on vision and contact, employ costly offline training procedures that need to be retrained for new environments and geometries. We propose BayesContact, a Simulation-Based Inference framework for visuo-tactile pose estimation in peg-in-hole insertion. BayesContact maintains a particle belief over object pose and fuses depth observations with force/torque-derived contact evidence. We employ simulation based forward models to approximate these observation likelihoods. For each pose hypothesis, a renderer predicts depth measurements and a physics simulator predicts contact outcomes under guarded probing actions; both are scored against real observations to update the belief. The resulting multimodal belief also enables information-gain-based probing for active disambiguation. Across simulated geometries and real-robot experiments, BayesContact improves pose observability and insertion success over vision-only inference by 30%

### [182] [VTLoc: Learning-based Tactile Contact Localization in Visual Point Clouds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16146)
*Zhiyuan Wu,Zhuo Chen,Shan Luo*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: VTLoc提出了一种视觉-触觉融合框架，通过几何多模态对齐模块和迭代定位更新器，利用3D点云作为视觉输入，实现触觉接触点在物体表面的精确定位，在100个真实物体数据集上显著提升了单点接触定位性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视觉提供全局物体上下文，触觉提供接触点的精确局部信息，但将两者融合进行接触定位面临跨模态空间对齐的挑战，需要准确建立触觉数据与视觉几何之间的空间对应关系。

Method: 提出VTLoc框架，包含两个核心组件：1) 几何多模态对齐模块（Geometric Multi-modal Alignment Module），从融合的视觉-触觉特征重建伪点云，并与视觉点云对齐以强制跨模态空间一致性；2) 迭代定位更新器（Iterative Localizing Updater），利用融合特征迭代优化预测的接触位置。

Result: 在包含100个真实物体的新基准数据集上，VTLoc有效减少了局部到全局的对应歧义，提升了单点接触定位的准确性。

Conclusion: 视觉与触觉的几何对齐是解决接触定位问题的关键，VTLoc通过显式空间对齐和迭代更新策略有效融合了两种模态信息。

Abstract: Vision and touch are complementary modalities essential for robotic perception and manipulation. While vision provides global object context, touch offers precise local information at contact points. Integrating these modalities for contact localization, i.e., predicting the location of touch on an object's surface, poses significant challenges due to the need for accurate spatial alignment between tactile data and visual geometry. To address this challenge, we propose VTLoc, a novel visual-tactile framework that localizes contact points from tactile readings using a 3D point cloud as visual input. VTLoc introduces two key components: a geometric multi-modal alignment module, which reconstructs a pseudo-point cloud from fused visual-tactile features and aligns it with the visual point cloud to enforce spatial consistencies across modalities; and an iterative localizing updater, which iteratively refines the predicted contact location using fused visual-tactile features. Evaluated on a new benchmark of 100 real-world objects, VTLoc improves single-touch contact localization by reducing local-to-global correspondence ambiguity.

### [183] [Vision-Language-Motion Maps: An Open-Vocabulary, Uncertainty-Aware, Queryable Motion Attribute for 3D Scene Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16173)
*Dibyendu Ghosh,Ayushi Shakya*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出视觉-语言-运动地图(VLMM)，一种开放词汇、自然语言可查询的3D地图，每个元素融合语义先验运动和几何观测运动，并附带不确定性，支持回答物体“能移动”、“正在移动”或“静止”三类查询。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放词汇3D地图假设静态场景，无法回答场景元素如何运动的问题。

Method: 每个地图元素携带融合运动属性：VLM/LLM语义可移动性先验 + 几何观测的跨帧运动，以及每个元素的不确定性。查询转化为属性过滤器，区分已观测移动、可能移动但未观测、静止三类。

Result: 在AI2-THOR模拟器上消融实验表明语义先验和观测运动不可相互替代；在TUM/Bonn真实动态RGB-D序列上，不确定性通道持续提升moving-vs-static平均精度，减少误报；后验等温校准后ECE达0.10。

Conclusion: VLMM是首个同时具备开放词汇、语言可查询、融合先验与观测运动、逐元素不确定性四个属性的3D地图表示。

Abstract: Open-vocabulary 3D maps let robots answer language queries about what and where, but they assume a static world and cannot answer queries about how scene elements behave. We introduce Vision-Language-Motion Maps (VLMM), an open-vocabulary, natural-language-queryable 3D map in which each element carries a fused motion attribute: a VLM/LLM semantic movability prior combined with geometrically observed cross-frame motion, together with a per-element uncertainty. Queries reduce to attribute filters that distinguish what has been seen to move, what could move but has not, and what stays still. On a controlled simulator benchmark with exact ground truth (AI2-THOR, three scene types) we show through ablation that the schema fields are non-substitutable: a semantic-only baseline fails motion queries even with strong features, and neither motion field substitutes for the other (the prior cannot answer "what is moving," observed motion cannot answer "what could move"). On real dynamic RGB-D (TUM and Bonn, six sequences) we show the uncertainty channel-our key difference from prior fused-motion work-consistently improves moving-vs-static average precision and reduces false motion flags, and is robust to estimated (noisy) poses. The raw confidence is not calibrated, but post-hoc isotonic calibration reaches an expected calibration error of 0.10. VLMM is a representation contribution: the closest prior maps each lack at least one of the four properties-open-vocabulary, language-queryable, fused prior-and-observed motion, and per-element uncertainty-that our combination provides.

</details>


### [184] [Handroid: Bridging Dexterous Hand and Humanoid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.16187)
*Ruogu Li,Chenyang Ma,Sikai Li,Zhenyu Wei,Yunchao Yao,Haochen Shi,C. Karen Liu,Shuran Song,Mingyu Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: Handroid是一款桌面级双形态机器人，通过重新配置同一套27自由度的机电本体，可分别实现灵巧手（20自由度仿人手）和桌面人形机器人（含12自由度下肢运动结构）两种形态，并提供了统一的控制与学习框架，支持灵巧操作、人形 locomotion、交互式动作编排及长时序任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上灵巧手和人形机器人作为不同形态独立发展，前者擅长物体尺度的接触丰富操作，后者提供以人为本环境中的移动能力和全身交互。作者旨在将两者能力融合于一个可重构平台，实现紧凑、可复现的双形态机器人系统。

Method: 通过设计一套27自由度机电本体，在灵巧手形态下20个自由度构成仿人手结构，在人形形态下重新配置为含头部、手臂和12自由度下肢的桌面人形机器人；同时构建统一控制与学习框架，支持遥操作、抓取、手中操作、locomotion、步态生成和交互式动作编排。

Result: 在真实世界中验证了灵巧操作、基于强化学习的 locomotion、关键帧动作部署，以及包含形态重构、移动、对接和灵巧抓取放置的长时序任务。

Conclusion: Handroid作为一种紧凑、可复现的平台，推动了形态可重构机器人学和跨形态机器人学习的发展。

Abstract: Dexterous hands and humanoid robots are typically developed as distinct embodiments: the former enable contact-rich manipulation at the object scale, whereas the latter provide mobility and whole-body interaction in human-centered environments. We introduce \textbf{Handroid}, a desktop-scale dual-embodiment robot that integrates both capabilities within a single reconfigurable platform. Handroid reuses one 27-DoF electromechanical body as either a dexterous hand or a desktop humanoid, measuring 0.33 m in height and 2.05 kg in weight. In the dexterous hand embodiment, 20 DoFs form an anthropomorphic hand closely matching the kinematic structure of the human hand. In the humanoid embodiment, the same articulated modules are reconfigured into a humanoid with a head, arms, and legs, including a 12-DoF lower-limb structure for locomotion and whole-body motion. Handroid further provides a unified control and learning framework supporting hand teleoperation, dexterous grasping, in-hand manipulation, humanoid locomotion, gait generation, and interactive motion authoring. We validate the platform through real-world dexterous manipulation, reinforcement-learning-based locomotion, keyframe motion deployment, and a long-horizon task involving embodiment reconfiguration, locomotion, docking, and dexterous pick-and-place. These results position Handroid as a compact and reproducible platform for advancing morphology-reconfigurable robotics and cross-embodiment robot learning.

</details>

### [185] [GraphDx: A Cost-Aware Knowledge-Enhanced Multi-Agent Framework for Sequential Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15280)
*Shaoting Tan,Ning Liu,Yuntao Du,Shuyue Wei,Wu Shuai,Qian Li,Yanyu Xu,Wei Zhang,Lizhen Cui,Haitao Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphDx是一个知识增强框架，通过构建医学诊断知识图谱（MDKG）和三个协作智能体（感知、推理、决策），将LLM的诊断成功率从50-68%提升至79-93%，同时将测试成本降低20-54%，解决了LLM在成本约束下难以系统推理的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM方法存在知识-推理鸿沟：虽然编码了大量医学知识，但在成本约束下难以系统推理，常常过度测试。

Method: 提出GraphDx框架，包含两个核心创新：(1) 自动化流水线构建MDKG，具有量化典型性、以动作为中心的拓扑结构和双目标属性（诊断相关性和成本敏感性）；(2) 三个协作智能体：感知智能体和决策智能体处理语言理解与生成，推理智能体在MDKG上执行确定性证据评分和成本感知规划。

Result: 在MedQA和MIMIC-IV数据集上，基于DeepSeek-V3、Kimi-k2、Llama-3.3三种LLM骨干，GraphDx将诊断成功率从50-68%提升至79-93%，测试成本降低20-54%。

Conclusion: GraphDx为自动化临床诊断提供了稳健、经济且可解释的解决方案。

Abstract: Sequential diagnosis requires balancing diagnostic accuracy against resource costs through iterative information gathering. Existing Large Language Model (LLM) approaches exhibit a critical knowledge-reasoning gap: despite encoding extensive medical knowledge, they struggle to reason systematically under cost constraints, often resorting to excessive testing. We propose GraphDx, a knowledge-enhanced framework with two core innovations. First, we design an automated pipeline that leverages LLMs to construct Medical Diagnosis Knowledge Graphs (MDKGs) with quantized typicality, action-centric topology, and dual-objective attributes for both diagnostic relevance and cost-sensitivity. Second, we introduce three collaborative agents (Perception, Reasoning, and Decision) where the Perception and Decision Agents handle language understanding and generation, while the Reasoning Agent performs deterministic evidence scoring and cost-aware planning on the MDKG. Experiments on MedQA and MIMIC-IV across three LLM backbones (DeepSeek-V3, Kimi-k2, Llama-3.3) show that GraphDx improves diagnostic success rates from 50--68% to 79--93% while reducing test costs by 20--54%, providing a robust, economical, and interpretable solution for automated clinical diagnosis.

### [186] [Causal-Audit: Explicit and Auditable Graph-based Reasoning via Target-Aware Causal Chain Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15281)
*Su Lan,Xuefei Yin,Yanming Zhu,Alan Wee-Chung Liew*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种显式且可审计的因果推理框架，用于无上下文的干预式问答。该方法通过目标感知的因果图构建和路径级因果证据聚合，在多个基准上优于现有LLM方法，并提供可解释的推理轨迹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的方法在因果和干预式问答中依赖隐式语言级推理，导致因果假设不透明、推理路径不可验证、预测脆弱，尤其在无上下文设置中表现不佳。

Method: 将因果推理形式化为四个模块化阶段的结构化推理：显式因果图构建（目标感知策略，以目标变量为核心约束抑制无关变量和虚假关系）、路径级因果证据聚合（组合多条因果路径，建模增强和抵消效应）。

Result: 在三个基准数据集上，该框架一致优于现有的基于LLM的方法，同时提供可解释和可审计的因果推理轨迹。

Conclusion: 显式结构化因果推理结合目标感知图构建和路径级证据聚合，能有效提升LLM在无上下文干预式问答中的鲁棒性和可解释性。

Abstract: Causal and intervention-based question answering is fundamental to advancing large language models (LLMs) toward reasoning beyond surface-level correlations and understanding underlying causal mechanisms. However, existing LLM-based methods often rely on implicit language-level reasoning, resulting in opaque causal assumptions, unverifiable reasoning paths, and fragile predictions under complex interventions, particularly in context-free settings. In this paper, we propose an explicit and auditable causal reasoning framework for context-free intervention-based question answering. Our method formulates causal inference as structured reasoning over an explicit causal graph through four modular stages, rather than implicit end-to-end prediction. A key innovation is a target-aware causal graph construction strategy that treats the target variable as a core constraint during graph expansion, effectively suppressing irrelevant variables, spurious causal relations, and reasoning noise. We further introduce a path-level causal evidence aggregation mechanism that combines multiple causal paths while modeling both reinforcing and counteracting effects, enabling robust decision-making beyond single-chain reasoning. Extensive experiments on three benchmarks demonstrate that our framework consistently outperforms existing LLM-based methods while providing interpretable and auditable causal reasoning traces.

</details>


### [187] [Cura 1T: Specialized Model for Agentic Healthcare](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15314)
*actAVA AI,:,Haolin Chen,Leon Qi,Steve Brown,Deon Metelski,Tao Xia,Joonyul Lee,Qixuan Wang,Kevin Riley,Frank Wang,Weiran Yao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Cura 1T是一个医疗专用大语言模型，通过人工把关的自我进化循环进行训练，在每个进化轮次中针对特定能力进行数据混合优化，从而在医疗评估套件中达到领先水平，同时保持跨领域推理和智能体基准的竞争力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗领域需要涵盖高风险沟通、专家推理和工作流执行等多种场景的专用LLM，但现有模型在这些用例上覆盖不足，且针对单一任务的更新可能导致其他能力退化。

Method: 提出人类把关的自我进化循环（human-gated self-evolution loop），每轮包含四个步骤：训练代理规划目标能力→训练模型→评估基准轨迹→从观察到的失败中精炼数据混合。该数据为中心的循环通过针对性的合成和精选示例改进模型，而非单一通用医疗数据更新。

Result: 在医疗评估套件中，Cura 1T在前沿基线中排名靠前或顶尖，同时在跨领域推理和智能体基准上保持竞争力。

Conclusion: 通过持续迭代的自我进化与数据混合精炼，能够在不牺牲通用能力的前提下提升医疗专用任务性能，验证了数据为中心的自进化训练范式在构建医疗专用LLM上的有效性。

Abstract: Healthcare spans high-stakes communication, expert reasoning, and workflow execution, yet specialized LLMs that cover these use cases together remain limited. A healthcare model must handle patient consultation, clinical reasoning over text and images, interactive diagnosis, and electronic health record (EHR) tool use. These capabilities fail in different ways, and a narrow update for one task can degrade another. We present Cura 1T, a healthcare-specialized LLM trained through a human-gated self-evolution loop. In each evolution round, a training agent plans a target capability, trains the model, evaluates benchmark trajectories, and refines the data mixture from observed failures. This data-centered loop improves the model through targeted synthetic and curated examples rather than a single generic medical-data update. Across the healthcare evaluation suite, Cura 1T ranks at or near the top among frontier baselines, while remaining competitive on out-of-domain reasoning and agentic benchmarks.

</details>


### [188] [AnovaX: A Local, Multi-Agent Voice Assistant with LLM Planning, Typed Executors, and Adaptive Recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15367)
*Raunak B Sinha*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AnovaX 是一个完全运行在用户本地计算机上的轻量级桌面语音助手，通过单个 Python 进程集成了唤醒词、语音流水线、LLM 规划器（Gemini）、安全层、多智能体编排器、自适应恢复循环以及手机远程控制功能，能够在不将音频传出设备的情况下完成打开应用、输入文字、运行搜索、协调并发动作和故障恢复等操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有桌面语音助手过度依赖云端流水线，将原始音频上传至服务器，且仅提供固定的有限技能集，缺乏本地优先、可扩展和透明可控的解决方案。

Method: 采用单进程 Python 架构，集成唤醒词门控、语音流水线、Gemini LLM 规划器（输出 JSON 格式工具调用计划）、白名单/黑名单安全层、多智能体编排器（将计划翻译为绑定线程池的带类型子智能体）、自适应恢复循环（ReAct 风格提示 + 只读工具的推测执行）。每个工具对应一个专业智能体类（AppAgent、TypingAgent、BrowserAgent 等），各有独立超时、重试策略和共享资源锁；支持递归 MetaAgent（最多两层嵌套）。配套 Flask 服务器通过本地 WiFi 提供手机友好远程界面，实时镜像智能体生命周期事件并流式传输笔记本屏幕（MJPEG）。

Result: 一个仅数千行代码的本地优先助手，能够打开应用、键入文本、运行搜索、协调并发动作、从单步失败中恢复，并完全通过同局域网内的手机远程驱动，整个过程无需 LLM 直接接触键盘。

Conclusion: AnovaX 证明了构建一个可理解、轻量级（数千行代码）的本地桌面语音助手是可行的，虽然不旨在与 Siri 或 Alexa 竞争，但在隐私保护、透明性和扩展性方面提供了有意义的替代方案。

Abstract: Desktop voice assistants are still dominated by cloud pipelines that ship raw audio off the machine and expose a fixed set of skills. We describe AnovaX, a small local-first assistant that runs entirely on the user's computer and treats the desktop itself as its action surface. A single Python process wires together a wake-word gate, a speech pipeline, an LLM planner (Gemini) that emits a JSON plan of tool calls, a whitelist-and-denylist safety layer, a multi-agent orchestrator that translates each plan into typed child agents on a bounded thread pool, and an adaptive recovery loop that takes over whenever a core step fails. Every tool corresponds to a specialized agent class (AppAgent, TypingAgent, BrowserAgent and six others) with its own timeout, retry policy, and shared-resource locks. A recursive MetaAgent lets the planner delegate a sub-goal back to itself, capped at two levels of nesting. The recovery loop uses a compact ReAct-style prompt and hides Gemini's latency behind speculative execution of read-only tools. A companion Flask server exposes a phone-friendly remote over the local WiFi, mirrors every agent lifecycle event to the phone in real time, and streams the laptop's screen back over MJPEG so the user can watch remote commands land as they run. The point of the project is less to compete with Siri or Alexa than to show that a legible, few-thousand-line assistant is enough to open apps, type into them, run searches, coordinate concurrent actions, recover from single-step failures, and be driven entirely from a phone in another room -- without the LLM ever touching the keyboard.

</details>


### [189] [Precise but Uncoupled: Reviewer Precision Does Not Guarantee Critique Uptake in Multi-Agent Math Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15388)
*Chih-Hsuan Yang,Jingyan Jiang,Vikram Vasudevan,Cheng-Hau Yang,Huihuo Zheng,Le Chen,Eliu A. Huerta,Venkatram Vishwanath,Ian T. Foster,Rajeev Thakur*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 在4181道Omni-MATH问题上测试发现，广播式讨论比规划-执行-审查（PER）流水线在困难问题上准确率更高。原因不在于审查质量（PER的审查者更精确，0.861 vs 0.644），而在于PER的批评更难促使答案改变，导致修复效果差。审查者中心的评估可能高估系统性能：能发现错误不等于能解决问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多数学与科学导向的智能体系统采用分层设计并设置专门的审查角色，假设审查阶段能够将错误候选转化为正确候选。本文旨在系统检验这一假设的真实性。

Method: 在4181道Omni-MATH问题上，使用gpt-oss-120b作为参与者，比较广播式讨论与规划-执行-审查（PER）流水线两种协作协议的性能，并从审查质量与批评对答案改变的驱动能力两个维度分析性能差异。

Result: 广播式讨论在困难问题上（tier4+）准确率显著高于PER；PER的审查者更精确（0.861 vs 0.644），但其批评更难促使下一轮候选答案改变，导致修复效果较差。强制显式ACK会降低PER准确率，而将审查指导嵌入求解器上下文可部分改善但无法消除差距。

Conclusion: 审查质量与批评采纳是经验上可分离的。以审查者为中心的性能评估可能高估系统质量：协议能发现错误并不等同于能解决更多问题，关键在于是否能将批评转化为有效的答案修正。

Abstract: Many math- and science-oriented agent systems use hierarchical designs with specialized reviewer roles, assuming that a dedicated review stage should help turn wrong candidates into correct ones. We test this assumption on 4,181 verifier-grounded Omni-MATH problems using matched gpt-oss-120b actors. Collaboration adds little on the easiest tiers, but from tier 4 onward the gains open sharply; in this harder regime, broadcast-style peer discussion reaches higher final accuracy than a planner-executor-reviewer pipeline (PER). We ask whether this gap is explained by reviewer quality or by whether critique changes the next answer the protocol carries forward. It is not explained by reviewer precision alone: PER's reviewer is more precise than broadcast's (0.861 vs. 0.644), yet evaluator-verified useful critique is much less likely to change the next candidate and produces lower reviewer-guided repair. These results show that reviewer detection quality and critique uptake are empirically separable. Within matched PER interventions, forcing explicit acknowledgment lowers final accuracy, while embedding reviewer guidance directly in the solver's working context partially improves follow-through without closing the gap. Overall, reviewer-centric evaluation can overstate system quality: a protocol may spot errors well yet still fail to solve more problems if it does not act on those critiques.

</details>

*Yoonhwa Jung,Junryu Fu,Mani Golparvar-Fard*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了DrawingVQA基准，首个评估多模态大模型在真实建筑图纸理解上的基准，包含33张施工图纸和92个问答对，覆盖三个推理深度。评估显示当前最先进模型与专家性能存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准多聚焦自然图像或简单示意图，缺乏对工程领域中复杂视觉-文本融合文档（如施工图纸）的评估，而施工图纸融合了几何、符号、表格、注释和领域文本，是工程工作流的核心媒介。

Method: 构建包含33张真实施工图纸和92个专家策划问答对的基准，采用三重推理深度（感知理解、上下文解释、领域专家推理）和双分类框架（七个工程维度+四个MLLM能力维度）进行系统评估。

Result: 当前最先进多模态大模型在施工图纸理解任务上，特别是高层次推理深度上，与人类专家表现存在显著差距。

Conclusion: 该基准为领域专用多模态推理奠定基础，促进AI理解与真实工程工作流的集成，揭示了当前模型在工程图纸理解上的关键短板。

Abstract: We introduce DrawingVQA, the first benchmark designed to evaluate multimodal large language models (MLLMs) on real-world construction drawings -- a core media in architecture, civil, and many other engineering practices. Unlike natural images or schematic floor plans, construction drawings fuse abstract geometry, symbolic notation, tabular data, annotations, and domain-specific text, forming a uniquely complex visual-textual domain core to engineering workflows. DrawingVQA bridges this gap with 33 "Issued for Construction" drawings and 92 expertly curated question-answer pairs, spanning three reasoning depths: perceptual understanding, contextual interpretation, and domain-expert reasoning. To evaluate model capabilities, we present a dual categorization framework to jointly analyze performance across seven construction-engineering and four MLLM capability dimensions -- the first to explicitly map engineering workflows to AI reasoning competencies. Evaluations of state-of-the-art MLLMs reveal a substantial gap between model and expert performance, particularly at higher reasoning depths. This benchmark lays a foundation for domain-specialized multimodal reasoning to allow for advancement on integration of AI-driven understanding and real-world engineering workflows.

### [191] [Do Coding Agents Need Executable World Models, Simplification, and Verification to Solve ARC-AGI-3?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15439)
*Sergey Rodionov*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过四个嵌套的Codex智能体消融实验，系统归因了ARC-AGI-3智能体中可执行世界建模、计划简化和精确回放验证三个核心组件各自对性能的贡献。主要发现包括：更强模型和更高推理努力普遍提升所有变体；各组件效果因设置而异；完整验证组合在所有设置中排名第一，但资源消耗显著更大；在最新模型上验证变体几乎完全解决了所有公开游戏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前构建的ARC-AGI-3智能体同时包含可执行世界建模、计划简化和精确回放验证三个组件，但各组件对最终性能的具体贡献不明确，需要系统归因来理解每种想法的实际效果。

Method: 设计四个嵌套的Codex智能体进行系统消融：文本基线（无世界模型）、灵活接口可执行世界模型（无回放验证）、带计划简化的可执行模型、带固定接口的完整验证（含简化和精确回放）。使用gpt-5.4和gpt-5.5在high和xhigh两种推理努力下评估，后续用gpt-5.6-sol在xhigh和max下探索。

Result: 更强模型和更高推理努力普遍提升所有变体；组件效果随设置变化：文本变体在gpt-5.5两个设置中优于灵活接口变体；简化在绝大多数设置中提升性能；完整验证在所有设置中排名第一但资源消耗大；在gpt-5.6-sol上验证变体几乎完全解决所有公开游戏（约99% RHAE，动作不到人类一半）。

Conclusion: 完整验证（含简化和精确回放）是性能最优的组合，但并非所有组件在所有场景下都绝对有益，尤其是可执行交付物并非普遍优于纯文本方法。在最新模型上接近饱和公开测试集，但需注意模型后见之明和未见数据的泛化问题。

Abstract: Our previous ARC-AGI-3 agent bundled executable world modeling, scheduled simplification, and exact replay verification, leaving unclear which idea accounted for its performance. We address this attribution question with four nested Codex-based agents: a textual baseline; a flexible-interface executable world model without replay verification; the same executable model with scheduled simplification; and a fixed-interface verification treatment that retains simplification and requires exact reproduction of recorded observations. The main study evaluates all four agents with gpt-5.4 and gpt-5.5 at high and xhigh reasoning effort on the public ARC-AGI-3 games. Exploratory follow-ups evaluate the textual and verification variants with gpt-5.6-sol at xhigh and max. The most robust result is that every agent variant improves with a stronger model and with greater reasoning effort. Within each model-effort setting, differences among variants are smaller than anticipated, while the effects of individual components vary across settings. Requiring a persistent executable deliverable is not universally beneficial: the textual variant outperforms the flexible-interface executable variant in both gpt-5.5 settings. Simplification improves performance in three of the four model-effort settings, with the weakest setting as the only exception. The complete verification treatment ranks first in all four settings, although it uses substantially more resources. In the gpt-5.6-sol follow-up, the verification variant fully solves every public game at both reasoning efforts, achieves about 99% RHAE, and uses fewer than half the total actions of the human baseline. Because the model postdates these games and held-out performance remains untested, this result should be interpreted as saturation of the public set only.

### [192] [Beyond a Joke: Multi-Angle Reasoning for Detecting and Explaining Harmful Humor in Memes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15442)
*Shanhong Liu,Pai Chet Ng,De Wen Soh,Malika Meghjani,Konstantinos N. Plataniotis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出MAR-12框架，利用视觉语言模型从12个结构化视角解读表情包，通过角色感知软门控注意力机制和原型分类器实现幽默与仇恨检测，在PrideMM和Memotion数据集上分别达到80.3%和75.9%的准确率，并生成可解释性强的推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态分类器要么忽视视觉、文本与文化语境的相互依赖关系，要么仅提供有限的可解释性，无法满足幽默、讽刺与有害意图并存场景下对可解释性表情包理解系统的需求。

Method: 1) 利用VLM从12个基于幽默与仇恨理论的结构化视角解读表情包；2) 采用角色感知软门控注意力机制学习各视角的贡献权重；3) 基于原型的分类器进行最终预测；4) 结合视角特定推理与注意力权重合成可解释输出。

Result: 在PrideMM和Memotion数据集上，幽默检测准确率高达80.3%，仇恨检测准确率达75.9%，均超越现有最先进方法；人工与GPT-4评估均确认生成的解释具有连贯性和说服力，尤其对幽默与有害线索共存的表情包效果显著。

Conclusion: MAR-12通过结构化视角推理与注意力机制有效解决了表情包中幽默与仇恨共存的复杂理解问题，在准确性和可解释性上均实现了对现有方法的全面超越。

Abstract: Internet memes intertwine visual cues, textual content, and cultural context, making them particularly challenging to interpret in scenarios where humor, sarcasm, and harmful intent coexist. These complexities highlight the need for explainable meme understanding systems that can provide reliable and structured reasoning to support both accurate classification and human interpretability. However, existing multimodal classifiers either overlook these interdependencies or provide only limited interpretability. In this paper, we introduce MAR-12, a novel framework that leverages Vision Language Models (VLMs) for meme detection and understanding in settings where humorous and hateful elements may coexist. The framework first interprets each meme through twelve structured perspectives derived from humor and hate theories. It then applies a role-aware soft-gated attention mechanism to learn how much each perspective should contribute, followed by a prototype-based classifier for the final prediction. Finally, explanations are synthesized using both perspective-specific reasoning and learned attention weights, ensuring transparent and context-grounded justifications. We evaluate MAR-12 on the PrideMM and Memotion datasets, where it achieves up to 80.3% accuracy for humor detection and 75.9% accuracy for hate detection, outperforming state-of-the-art approaches. Furthermore, both human and GPT-4-based evaluations confirm that MAR-12 produces coherent and persuasive explanations, particularly for memes in which humorous and harmful cues co-occur.

</details>


### [193] [From Black Box to Executable Logic: Explainable Reinforcement Learning through Prolog Expert Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.15459)
*Eduardo C. Garrido-Merchán*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将深度强化学习策略（黑盒）转化为可解释的Prolog逻辑程序的三阶段方法，包括策略提取、规则归纳和程序扩展，并提供理论保证（回报损失界、单调改进、终止性、逼近误差界）和实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度强化学习策略是黑盒模型，缺乏可解释性，无法被人类理解、逻辑引擎执行或优化器编辑。本文旨在通过将其转化为可执行的逻辑程序来解决这一可解释性问题。

Method: 三阶段后验变换：(1) 提取冻结的PPO教师策略；(2) 以经典关系学习方式从策略决策中归纳有序规则列表；(3) 将规则列表发射为Prolog程序，由现成逻辑引擎执行。后续扩展阶段编辑规则库，仅在策略评估确认回报提升时接受编辑。

Result: 在16,944个可达状态的两室钥匙门任务中，扩展后的Prolog程序在每种随机种子下均达到精确最优回报，且在预算受限下10/10种子超过随机教师。连续控制任务中，Acrobot用11条子句匹配教师（噪声范围内），CartPole恢复约97%回报，LunarLander仅部分恢复（符合指数下界预测）。

Conclusion: 本文证明了将深度强化学习策略转化为可解释逻辑程序的可行性，提供了完整的理论基础（四种保证）和实证验证，但受限于连续观测空间中决策边界的指数级复杂度下界。

Abstract: A trained deep reinforcement learning policy is a black box, and we ask whether it can be made explainable by rewriting it as an executable logic program that reproduces its behaviour and that a person can read, a logic engine can run, and an optimizer can edit. We present a three-stage post-hoc transformation that extracts a frozen proximal policy optimization teacher, induces an ordered rule list from its decisions in the manner of classical relational learning, and emits the result as a Prolog program whose every decision is executed by an off-the-shelf logic engine; a subsequent expansion stage edits the rule base and accepts an edit only when policy evaluation certifies a return increase. We prove four guarantees. A return-loss bound makes the distilled program a machine-checkable certificate in a finite Markov decision process, and the expansion loop improves monotonically and terminates. For the continuous-observation setting we answer whether the conversion is possible at all: the propositional threshold instantiation converts the network to arbitrary fidelity as the resolution B grows, with disagreement O(1/B) and a return gap that closes at the same rate, and a matching lower bound shows the cost is exponential in the observation dimension for an oblique decision boundary. Empirically, on a two-room key-and-door task with 16,944 reachable states the expanded Prolog program attains exact optimal return in every seed and, in a budget-capped regime, exceeds the stochastic teacher on exact return in ten of ten seeds. On three continuous-control tasks the emitted program substitutes the network, matching the neural teacher within noise on Acrobot with eleven clauses and recovering about 97% of its return on CartPole, while on the finer-control LunarLander it recovers only partially, exactly the ceiling the exponential lower bound predicts.

</details>
